| 0:23:55| What generally happens when we do the inspection,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=1435)|
| 0:23:58| we will ask for a current sprinkler inspection report from a state-licensed sprinkler contractor.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=1438)|

| 0:24:10| those then become deficiencies to our inspection.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=1450)|
| 0:24:14| NFPA 13, which is the code that governs sprinkler system,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=1454)|
| 0:24:18| does in fact require any obstruction to the sprinkler system greater than four feet,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=1458)|
| 0:24:23| and those ducts are greater than four feet, to be sprinkled underneath.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=1463)|

| 0:24:36| It's a four-by-four measurement.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=1476)|

| 0:37:58| I'd like to call on the Law Director.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2278)|
| 0:38:07| Mr. Chairman, we have researched all of the state statutes and looked at cases on this issue,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2287)|
| 0:38:17| and our independent research confirms what has been reported to us by.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2297)|
| 0:38:24| We also checked with both CTAS and MTAS to see if they had looked at these issues before,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2304)|
| 0:38:34| and they concur that in Tennessee there is a case, the Blazer case, that arose in Cocke County| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2314)|
| 0:38:46| where the county executive, and this is a Tennessee Supreme Court case.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2326)|
| 0:38:52| And without going into greater detail than need be, the end result is that when a public official| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2332)|
| 0:39:03| leaves office in the circumstances before us, then a replacement is chosen that if there is an appeal| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2343)|
| 0:39:19| and the appeal is successful, then the appellant is automatically entitled to go back into office.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2359)|
| 0:39:33| And whoever was appointed or even elected must vacate the office.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2373)|
| 0:39:42| In the case that I described to you, the Blazer case, after the elected official was forced out of office,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2382)|
| 0:39:55| the local legislative body appointed a successor.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2395)|
| 0:40:01| And then at the next regularly scheduled general election, that same individual stood for election| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2401)|
| 0:40:09| and was successful and was elected as county executive in Cocke County.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2409)|
| 0:40:18| But that next regularly scheduled general election where they were elected was still to fill the unexpired term.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2418)|
| 0:40:28| So the term of the county executive who had to leave office had not yet expired.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=2428)|

| 1:16:07| Mr. Chairman, I think it appropriate now to consider an amendment to this contract| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4567)|
| 1:16:15| because clearly we've been struggling to find a way to assure a spreading out of services.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4575)|
| 1:16:21| And we had a very good workshop with certain fair share provisions came into play in the discussion| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4581)|
| 1:16:28| and modeling this amendment after those is what I've done.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4588)|
| 1:16:32| So here's the wording I propose to be amended to the contract language.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4592)|
| 1:16:38| The party to this plan, known as the 10-year plan to end chronic homelessness,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4598)|
| 1:16:42| agrees that the next time it seeks funds under the control of Knox County for any project,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4602)|
| 1:16:48| that project must be outside the city limits of the City of Knoxville.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4608)|
| 1:16:51| Should the 10-year plan to end chronic homelessness fail in this regard,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4611)|
| 1:16:54| the money from this grant must be refunded to Knox County.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4614)|
| 1:16:58| I think this, in effect, says next time you come before us,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4618)|
| 1:17:01| come with something that spreads it out to a different part of our county.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4621)|
| 1:17:05| It's not zoning.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4625)|
| 1:17:07| It's a contract.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4627)|
| 1:17:09| It presents no issues of discrimination.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4629)|
| 1:17:12| I think it's a very reasonable provision that would hold this particular contract as a model| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4632)|
| 1:17:18| for how we spread out homeless services| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4638)|
| 1:17:22| and hold those who have spoken on this issue to their words to put homeless services in a variety of areas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4642)|
| 1:17:29| We have learned through that workshop that services can be brought to persons.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4649)|
| 1:17:33| Persons don't have to go to services.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4653)|
| 1:17:35| And so, therefore, I think it's a very reasonable thing to do, and I would move this amendment.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom081215?start=4655)|
